		}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = LKMT_china_state_tt
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_flag = LKMT_china_state
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GT_begonia_leaf"
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = LKMT_china_state
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					for_each_scope_loop = {
						array = global.countries
						if = {
							limit = {
								exists = no
							}
							remove_state_claim = PREV
							if = {
								limit = { check_variable = { PREV.core_countries^num > 1 } }
								remove_state_core = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_end_century_of_humiliation_tt
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL } 
	}

					}

				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = ETS
					decision = CHI_dec_negotiate_with_SIK_nation

			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = TAN }
				TAN = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = CHI
						modifier = CHI_national_autonomy
					}
				}

					target = TAN
					decision = CHI_dec_negotiate_with_SIK_nation
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = MON }
				MON = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = CHI
						modifier = CHI_national_autonomy
					}
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = MON
					decision = CHI_offer_autonomy_MON
				}

			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = TIB }

						target = CHI
						modifier = CHI_national_autonomy
					}
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = TIB
					decision = CHI_offer_autonomy_TIB
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ETS
						tag = TAN
						tag = MON
						tag = TIB
					}
					is_in_faction = yes
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				every_other_country = {

					}

						active = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
